Finding the Owner of All Things
 Today, as you all know, is the Day of All Things celebrated by our Unification Church. Before we commemorate this day, let us express our gratitude for the fact that we are welcoming a day when the sun and nature rejoice.
 God is the Subject of Our Love
 All people living in this world do not know where humanity comes from and where it is going. They simply believe that this life on Earth is the beginning and the end. They do not know who the owner of humanity is. When considering the value of that owner, they do not know what kind of owner it is. Furthermore, they do not know what kind of history humanity should pursue while being unaware of God.
 Consequently, they also do not understand the value or existence of all things apart from humanity. When viewed this way, questions such as why the sun exists, why the moon exists, and why humanity exists remain serious issues that need to be addressed throughout history. If there is anything that can provide a definitive answer to such questions among the countless people today, it would be none other than the Unification Church. (Applause)
 So how does the Unification Church speak of God? What do we think about God? We affirm that God definitely exists. Therefore, we do not just believe in God or know God; we understand God as someone we serve. What can we call that? And what is the conclusion? The conclusion is that God is the subject with whom we can have a loving relationship.
 Praising God with Love is the Highest Praise
 Now, what kind of love is that? It is a high-level love that cannot be explained with our intellect or reason. If spring is wonderful in this world, it cannot be compared to anything else in spring; if summer is wonderful, it cannot be compared to the best of summer, or to anything symbolizing autumn or winter. It is a high-level love that cannot be compared to any of these.
 Now, how happy would it be to experience such love and to possess such love? The expressions you use today, such as wonderful or great, cannot even begin to describe it. Can we express it through art, such as dance or song? That too would fall short. Then how will we express that joyful symbol? Will we lower our hands, or will we raise our hands and say "Ah"? It is not just raising our hands and saying "Ah"; we will express our amazement with everything, even down to our cells.
 Among all things, everyone knows that the sun is the element of life. When the bright morning sunlight spreads all around, everything under its influence—mountains, trees, the earth, even insects—welcomes it. Therefore, the sound of chirping birds receiving the bright sunlight feels different from ordinary bird sounds. Why is that? Because the subject—the bright light and the light of life—holds relative value, and because the beautiful shining sun is present in that land, it shines even brighter. Even the barking of a dog, which is usually unpleasant, does not feel unpleasant at that time under the morning sunlight.
 In that moment, all things praise the sun as the element of life, all chirping birds do so, animals frolic, and everything glorifies the sun, but if humanity does not understand this and simply stands there like "U-" (making a face), what will happen? What will happen? Historically, people have claimed that "humans are the crown of creation."
 If that is the case, then what is the center of all the beautiful bird songs or the sounds of all animals, no matter how brilliantly they shine in the glory of the sun? If there is no center, it will lead to a miserable outcome. If the center is humanity, then when a single human welcomes the sun and all things, everything will reveal its full value of glory.
 So, from the perspective of that center, who should respond first? Should the woman respond first, or should the man? "The man." (Laughter) It goes in order, so it is the women. When the birds chirp, the dogs bark, and when all things respond, then step by step, the women respond, and then the men are attracted to their beautiful faces. Why is that? Here, men have only gray suits, navy suits, and a few options, but women are colorful and diverse. Even from up here on the platform, I see that men have no interest, and my attention goes to the women first. (Laughter. Applause)
 Now, look at this. Under the brilliant sunlight, all nature responds, and it is fun and pleasant to sing, "Oh, shining sun! Beautiful nature! Whispering sounds of insects, flying butterflies!" Even if the environment is wonderful with the chirping of birds, can it compare to my voice and my expression of praise? (Applause) So, women sing and dance, and men respond by dancing as well. If in all of nature, the sun is to be the center, or if the birds are to be the center, it must be through the environment of those who are dancing and singing.
 Now, even if men and women dance, what is important? It is only in the place where they are intertwined and united with an unbreakable love that they connect the universe to express their joy and glory, and if they can praise before the high and noble God, who is the owner, that praise will be the highest praise.
 Living with God as the Subject of Love in the Unification Church
 Now, what would be God's hobby? What would God's hobby be? God can create nature at any time, can create sounds of songs at any time, can create people at any time; there is nothing He cannot do. He has the ability to do everything freely. So what is this? This is seen as a decorative item centered around love. It is a decorative item.
 However, if it is made as a decorative item of love but there is no object to love, then this decorative item becomes a condition of all resentment and a target of sorrow. It becomes a symbol of hatred, a symbol of hatred. If a husband buys a few-carat diamond for his beloved wife, he wants to show it off, but if there is no owner of that diamond, then that decorative item becomes a sorrowful decoration and a cursed decoration. It becomes a presence of hatred and a presence of curse. Do you understand? "Yes." Is that right? "Yes." That's right.
 Therefore, as mentioned earlier, we must serve God as the subject with whom we can relate through love, and we aim to understand and serve the profound heart of God. So, in this view, will God seek love or not? "He seeks it." God is also one who seeks love. So what about all things? "They seek it." In that sense, God is like a locomotive of love, while people are like passenger cars, and all things are like freight cars that will run along. (Laughter) When it runs through the heavens and orbits the earth and the universe, is there any being that would not be interested? "Everyone is interested." Anyone? "Yes." (Laughter) The answer is easy. Then what about those who are asleep? Those who are asleep will wish that someone would wake them up while they sleep. When they rub their eyes and wake up, will they want to go back or follow along? "They will follow." Where to? "Forward." So when the train passes, they just need to shout.
 In this view, why does the train run quietly? "I wish that as it comes, it would sound the siren and shout, and those who were sleeping would wake up and jump out." That is what I wish for the whole world. Normally, one might say, "Hey, this train, be quiet! I wish it would crash and overturn and break apart," but even if the ears are blocked, they still hear it. So, it is a wonderful place. (Applause) Today, sitting here in the heat... I could talk all day if I wanted to. But...
 To find the Kingdom of Heaven and live centered on God's love is to be a true person.
 Now, let’s think about this. If God's love is like that, where is that love? Where is it? "In people." That is because you are all members of the Unification Church. It is not in the traditional churches, such as Presbyterian, Catholic, Methodist, or in the White House where Carter lives... "No." Then where is it? "True Parents." Where are the True Parents? (Laughter)
 When we speak of that, if we focus on the word "true,"... the starting point of what is true is parents. Humans receive the blood of their parents centered on love... The term True Parents refers to the first parents, and we can conclude that it is based on that. (Applause) Do you understand what that means? That is why in the Unification Church, we talk about True Parents, True Family, True this and that. (Laughter)
 Then what does "true" mean? While the world walks this way, the Unification Church members walk the opposite way. That is how it is. It is upside down. Do you understand what that means? "Yes."
 However, the world is not going through the train of love; it is seeking material and everything else at the very end. So, in terms of trains, it is going to the last car. What is that last car? It is the toilet car for the passengers. (Laughter) What we in the Unification Church do is stop there and go straight to the locomotive.
 When we get there, is there a fragrance, is there smoke? This is not a place to sit and rest... So, all sounds come from there. The heartbeat resonates from there. This is a matter of life and death. But the feeling of conquering the world is alive. And I will be the first to arrive at the final destination; I am surely the first. I will be the first to reach the destination. Who will welcome me there? "God!" God will welcome me. God will say, "Here comes God." "God!" In Korean, "God" means a hat. (Laughter)
 In contrast, what do people in the world do when they go to the toilet car? They sit there... (gesturing. Laughter) And when they reach the destination, what happens? It becomes a big problem. Think about it. God will smell and say, "This guy is at the back of the train... But you who rode in the locomotive all sweated. Since that is the case, I will help you! Then those who rode in the passenger cars, come here. From now on, you will work as my sons and daughters. Amen." (Applause) This is a simple story, but in the world... (recording briefly cuts out) sitting here saying, "It’s coming! It’s coming! It’s coming! It’s coming! It’s coming!" Do you like that? "Yes." I like it too. Why? Because of God's love.
 We Unification Church members believe and know that we are not just going to live in the Kingdom of Heaven, but we want to find the royal palace of the Kingdom of Heaven and live centered on God's love. This motto is contained within. We want to live receiving love. We want to go to the royal palace and become part of the royal palace... Therefore, when there is a battle in a nation that can become such a nation, we must stand at the forefront of that fierce battle, and when there are difficulties, we must become people with the ability and experience to overcome all difficulties.
 If there is a couple among humans who can do that, they will all say "Amen" centered on love from the sun, all things, and God. God says Amen! All people say Amen! "Amen." Amen! "Amen." Do you know what Amen means? Amen means true person. (Laughter) A cool person is also Amen. (Applause) Amen means victory! Victory! Victory! Do you understand? I also like Amen. You all like Amen. God likes Amen. All things like Amen. Even the spirits like Amen. "Amen, Amen, Amen."
 So, do you like being a spirit? "Yes." What is a spirit needed for? It is needed for Sunie. A spirit is needed for the sun, isn’t it?
 Now, do you take pride in being a spirit? "Yes." In America, when Apollo 11 went, I don’t know if it was Armstrong or Legstrong, but they went to the moon. (Laughter) What are we? We are not Arm-strong, nor Leg-strong, nor Body-strong, but Heart-strong. (Cheers. Applause) That is why we are going to the land of the sun. If Armstrong went to the moon, then I am attached to the tail...
It is. That 'moon' refers to Reverend Moon. It means that I am attached to my tail. I am True Moon. That moon is... (laughter, applause) That is a joke. (laughter) So, do you understand how it feels now? You got the feeling, right? Young ones? (laughter)

Human history is a history of wars to build the bridge of love. 

Today, I am saying this. Why am I saying this...? God could not find that love, humans could not find that love, and all things could not find that love. God, as God, could not become the owner centered on that love in front of all creation, and humans, as the crown of creation, could not make contact with that love, and all things themselves have not yet formed a connection with that love. 

Humans have fallen. They have fallen to the very bottom of everything. So, we humans stand in front of all things, establishing them and standing there. To build that bridge, to play the role of that bridge, all things have come forth as sacrificial offerings before humans. In the process, all of humanity is competing with each other, holding onto each other, killing each other, and what are they seeking? An ideal world, a greater world, a more valuable world, and thus history has flowed out. 

The conclusion is that human history is a history in which countless people have sacrificed through the history of wars to build the bridge of love. In human history, as all things are sacrificed and countless humanity is sacrificed, in the end, there is one bridge to be built, and they are waiting for one person who can cross that bridge, which is the messianic thought, and the history of global Christianity has played the role of that bridge. 

From this perspective, the Messiah will come and represent humanity to cross that bridge. Then there is an order here; who should go first? The Messiah, who can receive the most of God's love, should go first, and then, according to the order of receiving love, others should follow. Isn't that the law that God sees? 

Now, then, if a person who has been fighting and being greedy until now sees the bridge that can conquer the world in heaven right in front of them, will they just stand still in front of that bridge, saying, "I will go in first, regardless of the Messiah"? 

Is that right or not? If that is the case, what will happen to that bridge? A time of confusion will come, a time of confusion. The world will be boiling, and there will come a time when this world cannot find direction and will be in chaos. 

Now, when we look at the historical era, you must understand that there has never been a time like this, where the world is in chaos and struggling to find a way to live. God, who knows that, cannot open the bridge wide and say, "Come quickly." There must be a person who possesses the key that can communicate that secret. 

When the people of Israel, all gathered together in the wilderness, fell into idolatry and chaos, Moses lifted up the bronze serpent. Those who looked at it, those who ran to grab it, lived. That is the war we are fighting. Similarly, God knew the bridge that the Messiah must cross, and instead of the bridges that the world is trying to cross, He created a new bridge. To cross that bridge, one must leap. One must know how to jump over the bridge. There is a rope that must be grabbed by crossing over the world and taking a risk. 

What is that rope? It is the snake rope. It is not a snake made like Moses' snake, but a living snake that flicks its tongue (gesturing). If you grab it, you die; there is no hope. Just touching it means death. Seeing that, everyone says, "Hee hee hee, if you go there, you will die. Don't go!" They are all in a frenzy... They say, "If you grab it, you will die!" but those foolish people who want to go towards that place are indeed foolish. (applause) If they say they will go, their parents will say, "You rascal!" and a kidnapping will occur. That is how they are being brainwashed. 

Do you like brainwashing? "No." I like it. (laughter) 

You must jump from there. On the day you jump, when you just grab it, everything will be okay. At that time, the living snake will wrap its tail around and lift it up onto the bridge before it falls. When you go up, there is the royal palace of heaven. And then you will take care of the world, saying, "I came here to save." 

You must run to the shining royal palace. 

When you kick the door open and go in, who is there? "Ha ha ha, my son, my daughter, welcome!" Who is that? It is our Father, God. How wonderful is that? Only then will it be said, "It is all accomplished." What Jesus said on the cross was not that. Only then will it be said, "It is all accomplished." What should be said to have been accomplished? It is not that all things of God have been accomplished. It must be said that God's love has been accomplished. Jesus could not do that. 

Then who is Reverend Moon? He was born as an instigator for such a nation. He is a global instigator, a leader of instigators. (applause) He is fiercely training the members of the Unification Church to place them there. Even while crying, they must not retreat; they must go forward, even while sweating, they must not retreat; they must advance, even while dying, they must advance, they must jump, and they must leap. 

Do you know about obstacle races? If there are obstacles in front, you must jump over them. It is okay if women run wearing only their underwear. It is okay if they run with their breasts out, as long as they run centered on love. When I go there, everything will be "Amen." (applause) So, when I come in and look quietly, my salvation is not the problem. I think of my mother and father. So now, I must build my own bridge, which is the family church of the Unification Church. (applause) 

All things want to meet the true owner who has love. 

Today is the day of all things, and these all things must seek something. Who do all things want to meet? They want to meet the true owner, the owner with love. Until now, what has happened? They have fallen into the possession of the evil satanic world and have acted as possessions of great ministers, then as possessions of princes, and then as possessions of servants. Everything has been ravaged as possessions of Satan. They have gradually lost their possessions and have fallen into the gutter. They have fallen into the place of utmost suffering. 

So what is the wish of all things? "Before God becomes the owner, if there is a person who is a servant of the servant sent from heaven before me, I wish to serve him instead of the owner." That is what they say. The path that humanity inherited as a tradition has been the path of religion. These things say, "I want to have once been a possession of the servant of the servant of heaven, and after that, I want to have once been a possession of the servant." They desire such things. 

They want to become the possession of God's servant of the servant, and then as a next wish, they want to become the possession of God's servant. What are they seeking? They are seeking the true owner, the true owner. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

Today, since we have gathered for the day of all things, the title becomes "In Search of the Owner of All Things." How much disdain would a servant of a servant receive? More than what humans suffer... The suffering that black people endure is several hundred times, several thousand times... This world is a world that has been wounded... because they are still proxy owners. They are false owners, proxy owners. 

Who are you? You are God's servants, you are God's adopted children. You are God's sons, you are the body of God that becomes God's temple? "The body of God." What is this? "The temple of God." Originally, you cannot come from that middle ground. You must start from the position of a servant of a servant. You have become that way because you entered the Unification Church. Even if white people disdain black people, you must be grateful if you are disdained here in the Unification Church. Then, it means you have "passed" and signed off. 

Unification Church members say, "Reverend Moon is all good, but I dislike Korean leader Park Bo-hee. I dislike Japanese leader Kamiyama. Oh, I dislike it..." "No, it is not." What is the Unification Church? It is a place to learn the law of indemnity. In my burden, there are burdens of the servant of the servant, burdens of the servant, and burdens of the adopted child. To take off these burdens and lead all people to take them off is the greatness of the Unification Church. 

That is why Reverend Moon knew that to find the love of the homeland, to find the world of love, one must go through this law of indemnity, so I played the game of being a servant of the servant. I played the game of being a servant, and I played the game of being an adopted child. You can go alone, but the teacher cannot. I must take all things with me and go this way. All things go, humans go, the spirit world goes... My whole life has passed carrying all burdens toward one purpose. Sixty years have gone by. 

Wherever love is centered, everything gathers. 

After graduating from college, after graduating from graduate school, and after completing the doctoral course, what is that doctoral degree? The only person in history who wrote a thesis centered on the theory of God's love and received a doctoral degree is Reverend Moon. What thesis did he write? He wrote a thesis on love. Therefore, to receive a degree on God's love in history, Reverend Moon's signature is needed. That is Reverend Moon's authority. The Unification Church becomes a museum that establishes bachelor's and doctoral degrees. 

That is why when they try to kill Reverend Moon and break this, heaven will kill them all. It is different. The Carter administration did all sorts of things to try to kill Reverend Moon... They want to see who can endure this. Why is there so much opposition to Reverend Moon? Because he is trying to create a museum of love. Why do people follow him around and take pictures everywhere he goes? Because of the museum of love, he draws crowds wherever he goes. 

That is why the Unification Church is said to be a church that does business and makes money. From the position of a servant of the servant, I will move you to the position of a servant, and from the position of a servant, I will help you cross to the position of an adopted child, and from the position of an adopted child to the position of a son, and from the position of a son to the position of parents, I will lay down the path to God. Therefore, all the businesses of the Unification Church are bound to develop. 

Look. When people gather centered on love, all animals gather, all of the universe gathers, and God gathers. Even the dogs in the neighborhood go to Bellvedere to relieve themselves. If all the neighborhood dogs relieve themselves in Bellvedere, the people living in Bellvedere will think our church is satanic. But that is not the case. While the dog is relieving itself, it says to its owner, "If you die, I will live in Bellvedere." (applause) Why is there a big dog house in Bellvedere? At that time, it will be full. 

So, all things, what is your wish? To go from the position of a servant of the servant to the position of a servant, to the position of an adopted child, to the position of a son, to the position of parents, to reach the heart of God's love, to fulfill the historical resentment before humanity, many sacrifices have been made... How much have you wanted to hear the words, "I tell you, from today, I will free you," and how many thousands of years of resentment has that been? You must understand that. Isn't that right? 

Who should be the owner of this world? Before the evil satanic devil becomes the owner, God must become the owner. Then, the ancestors of humanity who have not fallen on this earth, Adam and Eve, that is, the True Parents, must become the owners, and the family where true sons and daughters live must become the owners, and then the tribes, nations, and the world must become the owners. You must understand that this was the original ideal. 

Centered on this thought, God chose America, which must bear all global authority and take responsibility for the foundations of Japan, Germany, and the entire world, yet these guys have lost everything because they could not take responsibility. After World War II, it was hoped that America would even dominate the Soviet Union and enter the path of God's will, but these guys lost everything to the Soviet Union. They lost everything from Eastern Europe to Vietnam, India, and Korea. (The recording briefly cuts out) 

America was placed in the position of God's servant to prepare for the end when God's son comes to take over this world, but they lost everything. "Oh, America, you who let me fall into the hands of the enemy!" You must understand that the universe accuses them. If they do not listen, they will cut off your neck. They will cut off your parents' necks too... The communists will cut off your neck. They will take away your land, take away your possessions, take away your sons, and take away your life. 

Look. Why are all the big mansions of the Catholic Church and established churches being sold off today? It is because Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is buying them all. The entire Christian world must repent by holding onto Reverend Moon. They must repent. They must repent by holding onto their sons, their wives, and their husbands. After that, they will lose their sons, lose their wives, lose their husbands, and it will be a mess. They will lose everything, including themselves. These crazy people are messing around. They are messing around! 

So Reverend Moon is breaking everything here and making a new reform. He is annihilating everything that is decaying and making new prescriptions. They are making a fuss about doing this. What does it matter what university you graduated from if you are dying? What does it matter if you have a PhD from Harvard? If you are dying, what does it matter? If you have cancer, what does it matter? If your eye is blind and you think your eye is fine, and if your nose is crooked and you think your nose is fine, who recognizes that? God does not recognize it, the world does not recognize it, and Reverend Moon does not recognize it. 

They want it to perish, but it is growing bigger and bigger. Oh, there are a thousand people in my neighborhood, and among them, the only smart one is that person. (gesturing, applause) That is the problem. Oh, these enemies. I hate them so much. 

At first, my legs hurt, my hands hurt, my butt hurts, my head hurts, and my eyes hurt, but now, it hurts so much that I am dying, so I ask the members, "What medicine do you take to be so strong? Your eyes are strong, and everything is strong. What medicine do you take?" When they say, "I took the member's medicine," they will surely come to find out. We have the principle medicine. When it is administered, it is as sweet as honey, and it is good to take every day, whether it is one day, two days, three days, or four days. My eyes grow bigger, my mouth grows bigger, my hands grow bigger, and then I will say, "Oh, Reverend Moon is my teacher." That is the fuss. 

When that happens, the earlier members will not be able to keep up. It will definitely be that way. Reverend Moon is not stupid. He is smarter than you. That is why he is doing this. (laughter) 

The purpose of fundraising is to qualify as the owner of all things.
Why do I make you do fundraising? It is to qualify you as the owners of all things. Do you understand? Now, those who dislike fundraising are subject to the true accusations of all things, and because they do not qualify to own all things in the future, they will have to live difficult lives and be removed from this world. We do fundraising to become the owners of all things; is fundraising good or bad? "It is good." Raise your hand if you like fundraising. "Wow!" Raise your hand if you dislike it. Now, how many of you have never done fundraising until now? I urge you to do fundraising.

When the owner earns money, they put the money they earned and the principal into the safe. Do you understand what that means? People in the world give a tenth when they earn money, but we Unification Church members give a tenth, a hundredth, and even offer our own money. That kind of thinking is wrong. So where does that go? It goes into the treasury of the heavenly kingdom. How wonderful is that?

Now, when we ask whether the largest treasury in the heavenly kingdom is that of the Presbyterian Church, the Catholic Church, or the Unification Church, it is the treasury of the Unification Church. The treasury of the Unification Church is the largest, the most valuable, and the best. So who holds the key to that treasury? The key is held by Reverend Moon. Who opens it? Reverend Moon opens it.

I also contribute to that... If it were up to my greed, I wouldn't try to give less than what you have offered. I would want to give more, adding to what you have given; I never think about giving less. That’s how greedy I am. This is why I think, 'Only by ultimately possessing the qualification of the owner of all things can we find the path to becoming the owners of the human world.'

So, I talked about the train earlier; you have to go through hundreds of freight cars before you can get to the passenger car. As you go along, the noise gets louder, and Reverend Moon this and that... "Oh, this is so complicated! Oh, the noise is terrible! I should just quit..." The more you feel that way, the more everyone plans to kill Reverend Moon. They think about how to get rid of him, how to eat him up, roast him, cut him up... Then, who is riding at the very back of the locomotive? Champions who oppose the work of God are riding there. If they stay still, they will die; they will end up in prison...

If these kids charge forward, they will all disappear. If they try to charge, they will all vanish, and suddenly everything will turn around. They will jump over because of that. (Expressing with gestures. Laughter) You have to push! Do you understand? "Yes." That’s how the Unification Church operates. What do you think? "Great." Great or grave? Which is it? Which is it? Grave? "Great!" What is great about it? I don’t think so. Can you call it great? "Yes." Alright. It’s not grave. Do you understand for sure? (*From here, he speaks in English.)

The proclamation of the Day of All Things presents the qualification of the owner of all things. 

Now, we have learned this amazing fact that we have established the Day of All Things in human history. (Applause) Furthermore, in order to establish the image of the owner of fallen humanity, we have created home churches. That is why I said you should become tribal messiahs. What is a tribal messiah? It is the tribal parents.

The fact that the Unification Church has established God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and the Day of All Things is something that God, humanity, and all things have hoped for throughout history. You must understand that it is a commemorative day that has resolved all historical center points.

Today, the Day of All Things presents the concept and ideology of the qualification of the owner on this earth.

When I come to Belvedere, I say, "Ah, it feels good. Hudson River, New York, nature all around. I have appeared because you want to see the owner." I say, "If you make the sound of flowing water, I will hear it, and when the birds sing, the owner will hear it, and if an unknown bug or butterfly flies, I will be delighted by it. If there is sunlight, I will welcome it and praise you in glory." How wonderful is that? When I think like this, if there is a cloud that blocks the sunlight and makes me feel bad, I say, "Hey, cloud, you who have no owner protected by God's love, get out of the way," and it moves aside. To the birds singing in the garden, I say, "How much do you long for the love of the heart that can praise according to your original creation in the ideal of God's creation? I am the owner, so come and play with me," and they will come flying. Do you understand what I mean?

Our Tradition

When we talk about tradition, you may think of various things. The English respect tradition... Every country has something to inherit tradition. Any organization also needs tradition, and families also need familial traditions.

Humans live according to tradition centered on order and law.

When we look at religion, religions also have traditions, such as Judaism... The Jewish people respect tradition. You may remember the movie "Fiddler on the Roof," which respects tradition.

The Unification Church is the same. The Unification Church also needs tradition. Now, when we see this, just as our human world needs tradition, what about God if He exists?

When we consider the word tradition, we know that it has evolved along with the changes in history up to now. Then, can the path of tradition that the human world must follow or the path of tradition that the universe must follow or the path of tradition that heaven must follow be different? When we look at it this way, tradition is about what it is centered on and from where to where it goes.

When you look at the Chinese characters, the word tradition means something that has been passed down. The character "傳" means to inherit, and "統" means to connect or continue. The connection is not just any connection; it is made based on subjectivity. It is the character for "to lead." It means to continue based on subjectivity. There must be a strong subjectivity at work there. Then, when we look at the character for "to lead," what does it lead? It must connect to the whole.

When we look at the entire human world in this universe, we can understand that the entire universe moves, and all human life is centered around the movement of heavenly fortune. There, it must move based on order and law. It does not happen according to one's own heart; it happens according to tradition. This is how we see it.

Now, even when you look at your faces, where is the traditional place of the eyes that appear on your face? Here. The eyes must be in the middle of the face, and there must be two of them. The nose is like this, and the mouth is like this. This is tradition; it is an order that is set that way. Then what is the law? The eyes must blink and see; all of these are established as norms. That is how it is. The nose is for breathing, and the mouth is for speaking and eating.

Then, can the nose say, "Let's change that tradition; oh, this weight is always pulling me down, I can't live like this. The mouth is so much better, it just blocks and..." And can the eyes say, "Oh, I have to keep looking around 24 hours a day, I am going to wear out and die here"? Can they do that? When we look at this, the eyes are as they are, the hands are as they are... What would happen if these hands did not move? All of these exist according to the tradition of nature's laws and live by this survival tradition.

You all wear suits and clothes, but where did this clothing tradition start? The British started it! (Laughter) So, when the British and Americans fought, during the War of Independence, what clothes did they wear? The British wore suits, but the Americans must not have worn suits, yet they did. Even while fighting, they wore the clothes made by their enemies, whom they hated.

When we look at the act of wearing clothes, wearing convenient clothes belongs to tradition. Whoever started it has a subjectivity that represents the whole, so we can argue that we cannot oppose conforming to it.

When we look at the universe, what is the level of that tradition? Eastern people see it as heaven, earth, and humanity (天地人). With this title, when the whole enters into a family where this one subject relates, what happens? The father represents heaven, the mother represents earth, and the children represent humanity. This is how they connect. Does that seem right? "Yes." How, how is it right? "As Father said..." (Laughter)

Then what does that tradition do? The word "統" means to lead and create one. It means to gather everything and make it one.

In this concept, there are heavenly people, earthly people, and human people. This is how we see it. So, who is a heavenly person? This is someone who purely thinks of the way, thinking only of the divine, apart from the human world. Then who is an earthly person? An earthly person is someone who thinks only of earthly things. They live like animals without ideals or anything. Then who is a human person? This is a conscientious person. This is someone who speaks of conscience. They are in the middle layer.

When we look at people in this way, we can see plus people, minus people, and plus-minus people. However, we must not think that the combination of both plus and minus is greater than the plus.
You need to understand that this is a reflective entity connected to these two worlds. When viewed this way, a person can be seen as a representative of the universe, standing in the central position that combines heaven and earth. This concept emerges. Therefore, heaven tries to enter into people, and the earth also tries to enter into people. So, is a person like that? Yes, a person is like that. From this, we conclude that a person has three great parents: the heavenly parent, the human parent, and the earthly parent. Is that correct? Yes, it is correct.

Where did your body come from? "From the earth." It came from the earth. Then, where did the mind within this body come from? Where did the soul come from? "From heaven." That's right. It came from heaven. Next, where did your conscience come from? "……" It resembles your mother and father. It resembles heaven, it resembles your mother and father, and it resembles this earth.

Why do you have hair on your body? Why do you have hair? This earth has trees and grasses. It resembles them. When you look at Western people's eyes, you think, "Ah, they look like lakes." (Laughter) When you see the eyes of people with bulging eyes, it seems like waves are moving. Also, if we talk about the nose, the nose looks like a mountain. It resembles a mountain range, it looks like a mountain. And the mouth symbolizes flat land. "Um-" (making a facial expression) That refers to the horizon, the line.

You resemble your mother and father. In the principle, it says there is skin, a layer of skin, a layer of fat, a skeletal layer…. It is structured like the earth. There are bones and even bone marrow inside…. The furnace in the middle of the earth is like the bone marrow. Then there are the layers of rock, then soil, and then combined with water, it becomes something like oil; it is all structured like that. If you combine all the flesh-like soil, water, and such, it becomes something oily, which serves a lubricating function. It resembles them.

Who do you resemble? It may seem like you are just a mix of things, but you resemble your mother and father. Whether it's your mother's features or your father's nose, you resemble them all. (Laughter) In that resemblance, one eye may resemble your mother, and the other eye may resemble your father. That would be ideal. (Laughter) One hand resembles your father, and the other hand resembles your mother. It seems good to think that way, but there also needs to be order in all of that. If the eyes resemble each other, they resemble this way, and the nose resembles this way, and the mouth resembles this way, and the hands resemble this way. That is tradition. And when people walk, they walk like this. (Imitating) Why do they walk like this? That is tradition. It is all structured like that. It is not just random.

Now, this body resembles the form of the earth and resembles the mother and father. This is the principled position. After resembling the mother and father, who do you resemble? You resemble God. Who do you resemble? "God." Do you have a conscience? "Yes." Have you seen it? Have you touched it? "No." Have you tasted it? (Laughter) How is it? Is the conscience soft, rough? Then, is it good to just sit still? No, that is also undesirable. It would be nice if everything resembled each other well.

Then what do you want to resemble? This is how the concept of "I" is established. The necessity of prayer. 
In general, religions center their lives around prayer, and the Unification Church also lives its life centered around prayer. It’s the same. 
The reason humans need prayer is that they have fallen.

The world of good and evil and indemnity

Do you understand what the world of good and evil means? You all know what the world of good and evil is.

Relative relationships are established in giving to each other. 

Generally, it is thought that everything is relative. If there is a man, there is a woman, and everything is relative like that. The animal world is like that, the plant world is like that… When you look at it that way, everything is…
This is the concept that one comes to have. However, there are people who view the concept of good and evil in this way, both in terms of good and evil. Here, we come to think that a relative relationship recognizes the existence of opposing entities and can provide relative value to them. Ultimately, what this means is that one cannot assert absolute authority centered on oneself. Furthermore, we think that in the shared space between two, we pursue a higher value, a single purpose.

Now, when we look at our young men and women, we feel that as they enter adolescence, the demand for the other becomes stronger than their own assertion. What this means is that they try to see the other as more valuable while diminishing themselves, trying to regard the other as more precious. There is this tendency. Those who truly love each other inevitably ask each other, "How much do you love me?" The answer they seek is that they love more than anything else. They want that kind of answer. Moreover, they often ask, "More than your own life?" Only when the answer is "Yes" do they feel satisfied.

At the same time I answer that way, I also hope that the person asking will answer me in the same way. Do you understand what that means? The conclusion is that this is not a position centered on oneself but a position for the other. It comes from respecting the other and recognizing their value. We can catch this concept here. The desire for such answers centered around love means that if love is the center of the whole, then the world related to that love must also result in that way. Only then can such subjects move in harmony. They will move in harmony.

From this perspective, of course, people think of themselves, but before thinking of themselves, they think of the whole, the public, the nation, the world, and higher ideals. They think of something better. Even if there are two people in love, it cannot be just about them. They come together to pursue something else. We feel that we are in this position realistically. We are experiencing this in reality. Especially in a country like the United States, the world is one world, and one cannot live outside of this world. We have entered an era where we can feel that no one can live isolated from relative relationships on a global stage. The same goes for the communist world. Ultimately, it comes down to how to harmonize with the world. 

Why do we say the Soviet invasion of Afghanistan is bad? What is bad about it? It is a principle that the strong invade and dominate the weak. If we see it this way, there is nothing bad about it. From this perspective, what is bad about the United States?

Now, the question is how the concept of good and evil is structured. What we need to understand here is that while everything appears to be in relative relationships, in those relative relationships, it is not centered on oneself but rather on the other. It is about following the other while the other is central, and one is secondary. Based on this concept, we can measure the standards of good and evil.

Individual purpose for completion and overall purpose
We can understand this. The logic that two become one and establish a relationship is for a greater plus. The combination of minus and plus is for a greater plus. The greater plus and minus combine for an even greater plus. (While writing on the board) 

We can establish this formula, this logic here. After going to elementary school, one must go to middle school, then to high school, then to university, and then continue on. Everything from elementary school must unite and harmonize so that I can have relative value to rise above. That is correct. Therefore, to establish this logic, we must think of the relative world. (Pointing to what was written on the board)

From this perspective, the individual purpose and overall purpose spoken of in the Unification Church can be asserted based on a historically valid logical foundation. Then, what is the individual purpose? It is for individual completion, and what is the overall purpose? It is for overall completion. Therefore, it is correct to say that one cannot approach the overall purpose without completing the individual purpose. 

That is why, if America says, "America itself is enough. If we have this much, we can live well. We can live disconnected from the world," that cannot be the case. However, if we apply this concept one by one, everything fits. Even when looking at cells, it is all the same. Every cell in the human body fits perfectly.

If there is this logic, how far will it continue? How far will it go? It will continue infinitely. That is correct. It will continue infinitely. Then, what will be the purpose of the direction it is heading? If it is infinite, does that infinite move infinitely, or does it stay still? It moves. Then, will that movement be in a straight line or a circle? Some say straight, while others say circle. "It is a circle." Why is it a circle? Because a starting course is necessary… It is simple. Why is it a circle? Because it involves the ideology of subject and object, the direction cannot be anything but a circle. This conclusion arises. Do you understand?

It seems like they are going around randomly, but in the end, how does it settle? It forms a core. That is how it happens. The movement must form a central core while following along. Does that seem correct? "Yes." There is no such thing as straight-line movement. It is always curved movement.

Through logical reasoning centered on the actions of this world and relative relationships, we can derive a single concept. In this context, the essence of God's desire is not just to be loved in a superficial manner but to establish a relationship based on true love, which is characterized by order, purpose, and mutual respect. So when I go, there will always be a chicken ready to be caught. (Laughter) Don’t you want to eat a bit? So you want to follow the Teacher? Wherever I go, wherever I go… That has been the tragic path of the Unification Church until now. In the future, scholars will say, "Ah, Teacher, please come to our house. We will host you at our house." Isn’t that good? Isn’t that bad? "It is good." I thought it was good, but then such bad things happened. Is it good or bad? "It is good." Is it good? "Yes." I thought it was different?

Compared to the suffering I have endured, it is nothing. God knows that it is good and encourages me. The members of the Unification Church also let me know that it is good, so I have no choice but to accept it as good. If I think of the suffering, the shame, and the resentment, there would be too many wrinkles to smooth out. I have lived with such stories.

Therefore, the path I will take in the future is not only to become the owner of a palace but also to be a king, a president… Recently, when I tried to meet the president of a certain country, I had to investigate how to do it, but now they will come to find the Teacher. I do not know if that is my delusion or fantasy, but it seems likely. Do you understand? "Yes."

Let me tell you one story. At the scientists' conference… In Germany, for example, they invite 20 people each time, and around 500 or 600 people compete to be invited. The scholars who want to go are world-renowned individuals. These people are cut off mercilessly by young fellows like Kim Gye-hwan. So they came to me. And they are doing that. So, since the chairpersons came to the scientists' conference, they are all… But these Korean people… Is there anything special about Korean people? Korean professors also come here because I invite them.
I invited Japanese people as well, but I didn't invite any Western professors. Still, they don't complain, saying, 'Why weren't we invited?' They understand that even if they want to meet the chairman, it's common sense that he won't meet them. They think, 'That person is busy, so he can't meet us.'

But the Unification Church members, you see, they just come into Cheongpa-dong and wag their tails around. The person who should be greeted should decide, but the one who is greeting is deciding. (Laughter) It's ridiculous. The person who should be greeted should say whether to come in or not, but the person who is greeting decides to come in. That's how it is. (Laughter) 'You fools, you ignorant ones!' They don't chase them away but say, 'Oh, you came?' They don't understand this value.

Look. In Japan, they now call Reverend Moon 'Teacher Moon.' Do you understand? Yes. In the past, he was called 'Moon Seong-myung.' (Laughter) But now, when they see him, they say, 'Teacher Moon is a teacher born from Asia.' They say he was born from Asia rather than Korea. Why? Because that's how Japan can get involved. (Laughter) It's really interesting. If you go into a small shop and ask anyone about Teacher Moon, they say, 'He is not only from Korea but from Asia.' He is that famous.

Let's run breathlessly, betting our fate on the Unification Church.
Now, people traveling to America who don't know Reverend Moon from the Unification Church will be in real trouble. When they ask where you're from and you say 'Korea,' they'll ask, 'Do you know Teacher Moon?' If you say 'I don't know,' it's a problem. Letters addressed to 'New York, Reverend Moon' come in immediately. You don't need silly addresses. (Laughter) Now, if you say 'America, Reverend Moon,' it comes in right away. How convenient is that? (Laughter) The world is really convenient.

That's why there are so many unnecessary letters! You need to understand that. This is about doing home church activities, so why are you making a fuss about meeting the teacher? Recently, a district leader came from the local area and said, 'Teacher!' I thought he was calling me affectionately, expecting something interesting or that he would treat me to lunch, but when I asked, 'What's wrong?' he said, 'Won't you come to the local area?' He wanted me to go to the local area. I'm busy. Then he said, 'You must come to our district at least once. If you don't come, it won't do.' I said, 'Oh, really? We'll see, you little rascal.'

The Unification Church members are bold. (Laughter) They are really bold. They have no manners, no sense of style, and they are bold. Why is that? Sometimes, when I think about it, I feel a bit sad. 'These ignorant kids, they grew up without a father, as children of a widow,' I sometimes think. While thinking that, I wonder why I taught them incorrectly, and I take all the responsibility. Why did I teach them about True Parents? If a child comes to the house of True Parents, if they are a true child, they have the right to kick down the door and come in even if the door is locked at night. That's why I repent. 'Why did I teach the name True Parents? Because of the sin of teaching that name, I must be indemnified.' 

I'm not saying this because I want to right now; I'm saying that it's good for you to come, but you must do all your work first. Do you understand? This is about not being able to do your work and then showing up to receive treatment as a child, making your father embarrassed. It's ridiculous that you show up without doing your work and expect to be treated like a child. You should do all your work and then say you want to be treated like a child. Do you understand? Yes.

There are still remnants of such things. So even when I meet you now, I can't do as I please. If I could give you an award on behalf of God, what would I give? If there is someone who has made a name for themselves globally through home church, I would want to give them the best award.

Who will receive the first prize? It would be a Korean person…. Greedy Moon, whoever that is, still thinks that this unpleasant Korean person, whom I always curse and make suffer the most, is the one I want to see succeed. Even though they are unpleasant and like an enemy to me, if they can't do this….

So, who would be best to do home church first? Still, in my heart, I think it should be a Korean person. I ask you. It should be a Korean person. This is honest talk. Do you think so? You understand that, right? Yes. What that means is that I hope that such a person will come out soon. You need to know this. Do you understand? Yes.

So this morning, you should keep 'the Unification Church and me' in your hearts and run breathlessly to determine your fate. As you stand at the threshold of the finals, I hope you move one step faster and achieve victory easily, receiving the crown of glory. Do you understand? Yes.

[Prayer]
No one knew the sorrow of the Father’s heart as He looked upon the peaks of history that returned in failure. Father, in the distant past, when you had the ancient nation of Israel in your heart and called the family of Jacob to start your providence, after going through the era of Moses, the era of Jesus, leaving behind the bloodstains of Christian martyrdom, and the traces of the miserable history of the Unification Church, you have allowed us to remain here today without collapsing or perishing. I thank you once again for your hand of connection.

I remember 30 years ago, when I struggled in my twenties to help heaven. The tears, blood, and sweat woven together through the hardships I faced to establish my purpose have become like a panorama. To stand this nation before your will, I set the final conditions, even as the nation opposed heaven…. Even as I was trampled upon as a mere individual, treated like the enemy of the nation and the enemy of the people, I endured with deep emotional connections. Because you are alive, I did not perish even in a place where I should have perished, and I cannot help but thank you for the touch of your hand.

Before evening comes, I must surely fulfill your will and offer it to you, pledging to walk the path of victory. Father, when I think of these unforgettable historical stories, I know well that you understand the true intentions of Satan, who stands in the emotional position of avoiding Moon. I must walk the path you walk, and I know well that if I do not walk the path of True Parents, humanity will perish.

Father, although their steps toward home church are in a limited environment, they are walking a path intertwined with tears at the crossroads of sorrow. There is still a path of tears that must be advanced to weave home church, where homes share the same heart. I believe that your hand, which has been with us until now, will continue to be with us. Therefore, I know that we can overcome the difficulties we face, so Father, please be with us.

This morning, I spoke under the title 'The Unification Church and Me.' The Unification Church and we appear as a fateful path that cannot be severed. In the past, having lost our parents, we must resolve the historical grievances and the circumstances of restoration, going through the content of indemnity, and we must know that the descendants of the fall must walk this path with grievances, so I earnestly hope and wish for your blessings.

I thank you for allowing me to spend these days. Today, there is again a direction of heart that your will desires. May I and the future generations advance on the path of the Unification Church, the path of the Father, and may we be able to advance with all our hearts, energy, and sincerity, expressing gratitude, and may we become your proud sons and daughters who can receive your deep love.

I know that the Unification Church can manifest as glorious victors of heaven and earth, so until that day, may we not die, not fall, and may we be children who fight and win.

At this time, for this place, children of unification scattered around the world are offering their sincerity, and family members abroad are offering their sincerity for this time and place, especially praying for the situation in Korea and the situation in America. This morning, I hope that the path of the children of the Father can be promoted and shortened to seek the best way.

May the glory of that day be with you, with the Master, and with me, and may the day of victory for home church be realized. I bless all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. *
